    57	func cacheEntryExpiration() time.Duration {
    58	        r := rand.Intn(int(nbcache.DefaultIDPCacheExpirationMax.Milliseconds()-nbcache.DefaultIDPCacheExpirationMin.Milliseconds())) + int(nbcache.DefaultIDPCacheExpirationMin.Milliseconds())
    59	        return time.Duration(r) * time.Millisecond
    60	}

    62	type DefaultAccountManager struct {
    63	        Store store.Store
    64	        // cacheMux and cacheLoading helps to make sure that only a single cache reload runs at a time per accountID
    65	        cacheMux sync.Mutex
    66	        // cacheLoading keeps the accountIDs that are currently reloading. The accountID has to be removed once cache has been reloaded
    67	        cacheLoading         map[string]chan struct{}
    68	        peersUpdateManager   *PeersUpdateManager
    69	        idpManager           idp.Manager
    70	        cacheManager         *nbcache.AccountUserDataCache

    80	
    81	        // singleAccountMode indicates whether the instance has a single account.
    82	        // If true, then every new user will end up under the same account.
    83	        // This value will be set to false if management service has more than one account.
    84	        singleAccountMode bool
    85	        // singleAccountModeDomain is a domain to use in singleAccountMode setup
    86	        singleAccountModeDomain string
    87	        // dnsDomain is used for peer resolution. This is appended to the peer's name

    98	        metrics telemetry.AppMetrics

   103	        updateAccountPeersBufferInterval atomic.Int64

   106	// getJWTGroupsChanges calculates the changes needed to sync a user's JWT groups.
   107	// Returns a bool indicating if there are changes in the JWT group membership, the updated user AutoGroups,
   108	// newly groups to create and an error if any occurred.
   109	func (am *DefaultAccountManager) getJWTGroupsChanges(user *types.User, groups []*types.Group, groupNames []string) (bool, []string, []*types.Group, error) {
   110	        existedGroupsByName := make(map[string]*types.Group)
   111	        for _, group := range groups {
   112	                existedGroupsByName[group.Name] = group
   113	        }
   114	
   115	        newUserAutoGroups, jwtGroupsMap := separateGroups(user.AutoGroups, groups)
   116	
   117	        groupsToAdd := util.Difference(groupNames, maps.Keys(jwtGroupsMap))
   118	        groupsToRemove := util.Difference(maps.Keys(jwtGroupsMap), groupNames)
   119	
   120	        // If no groups are added or removed, we should not sync account
   121	        if len(groupsToAdd) == 0 && len(groupsToRemove) == 0 {
   122	                return false, nil, nil, nil
   123	        }
   124	
   125	        newGroupsToCreate := make([]*types.Group, 0)
   126	
   127	        var modified bool
   128	        for _, name := range groupsToAdd {
   129	                group, exists := existedGroupsByName[name]
   130	                if !exists {
   131	                        group = &types.Group{
   132	                                ID:        xid.New().String(),
   133	                                AccountID: user.AccountID,
   134	                                Name:      name,
   135	                                Issued:    types.GroupIssuedJWT,
   136	                        }
   137	                        newGroupsToCreate = append(newGroupsToCreate, group)
   138	                }
   139	                if group.Issued == types.GroupIssuedJWT {
   140	                        newUserAutoGroups = append(newUserAutoGroups, group.ID)
   141	                        modified = true
   142	                }
   143	        }
   144	
   145	        for name, id := range jwtGroupsMap {
   146	                if !slices.Contains(groupsToRemove, name) {
   147	                        newUserAutoGroups = append(newUserAutoGroups, id)
   148	                        continue
   149	                }
   150	                modified = true
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        return modified, newUserAutoGroups, newGroupsToCreate, nil
   154	}
   155	
   156	// BuildManager creates a new DefaultAccountManager with a provided Store
   157	func BuildManager(
   158	        ctx context.Context,
   159	        store store.Store,
   160	        peersUpdateManager *PeersUpdateManager,
   161	        idpManager idp.Manager,
   162	        singleAccountModeDomain string,
   163	        dnsDomain string,
   164	        eventStore activity.Store,
   165	        geo geolocation.Geolocation,
   166	        userDeleteFromIDPEnabled bool,
   167	        integratedPeerValidator integrated_validator.IntegratedValidator,
   168	        metrics telemetry.AppMetrics,
   169	        proxyController port_forwarding.Controller,
   170	        settingsManager settings.Manager,
   171	        permissionsManager permissions.Manager,
   172	) (*DefaultAccountManager, error) {
   173	        start := time.Now()
   174	        defer func() {
   175	                log.WithContext(ctx).Debugf("took %v to instantiate account manager", time.Since(start))
   176	        }()
   177	
   178	        am := &DefaultAccountManager{
   179	                Store:                    store,
   180	                geo:                      geo,
   181	                peersUpdateManager:       peersUpdateManager,
   182	                idpManager:               idpManager,
   183	                ctx:                      context.Background(),
   184	                cacheMux:                 sync.Mutex{},
   185	                cacheLoading:             map[string]chan struct{}{},
   186	                dnsDomain:                dnsDomain,
   187	                eventStore:               eventStore,
   188	                peerLoginExpiry:          NewDefaultScheduler(),
   189	                peerInactivityExpiry:     NewDefaultScheduler(),
   190	                userDeleteFromIDPEnabled: userDeleteFromIDPEnabled,
   191	                integratedPeerValidator:  integratedPeerValidator,
   192	                metrics:                  metrics,
   193	                requestBuffer:            NewAccountRequestBuffer(ctx, store),
   194	                proxyController:          proxyController,
   195	                settingsManager:          settingsManager,
   196	                permissionsManager:       permissionsManager,
   197	        }
   198	
   199	        am.startWarmup(ctx)
   200	
   201	        accountsCounter, err := store.GetAccountsCounter(ctx)
   202	        if err != nil {
   203	                log.WithContext(ctx).Error(err)
   204	        }
   205	
   206	        // enable single account mode only if configured by user and number of existing accounts is not grater than 1
   207	        am.singleAccountMode = singleAccountModeDomain != "" && accountsCounter <= 1
   208	        if am.singleAccountMode {
   209	                if !isDomainValid(singleAccountModeDomain) {
   210	                        return nil, status.Errorf(status.InvalidArgument, "invalid domain \"%s\" provided for a single account mode. Please review your input for --single-account-mode-domain", singleAccountModeDomain)
   211	                }
   212	                am.singleAccountModeDomain = singleAccountModeDomain
   213	                log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("single account mode enabled, accounts number %d", accountsCounter)
   214	        } else {
   215	                log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("single account mode disabled, accounts number %d", accountsCounter)
   216	        }
   217	
   218	        cacheStore, err := nbcache.NewStore(ctx, nbcache.DefaultIDPCacheExpirationMax, nbcache.DefaultIDPCacheCleanupInterval)
   219	        if err != nil {
   220	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("getting cache store: %s", err)
   221	        }
   222	        am.externalCacheManager = nbcache.NewUserDataCache(cacheStore)
   223	        am.cacheManager = nbcache.NewAccountUserDataCache(am.loadAccount, cacheStore)
   224	
   225	        if !isNil(am.idpManager) {
   226	                go func() {
   227	                        err := am.warmupIDPCache(ctx, cacheStore)
   228	                        if err != nil {
   229	                                log.WithContext(ctx).Warnf("failed warming up cache due to error: %v", err)
   230	                                // todo retry?
   231	                                return
   232	                        }
   233	                }()
   234	        }
   235	
   236	        am.integratedPeerValidator.SetPeerInvalidationListener(func(accountID string) {
   237	                am.onPeersInvalidated(ctx, accountID)
   238	        })
   239	
   240	        return am, nil
   241	}
   242	
   243	func (am *DefaultAccountManager) startWarmup(ctx context.Context) {
   244	        var initialInterval int64
   245	        intervalStr := os.Getenv("NB_PEER_UPDATE_INTERVAL_MS")
   246	        interval, err := strconv.Atoi(intervalStr)
   247	        if err != nil {
   248	                initialInterval = 1
   249	                log.WithContext(ctx).Warnf("failed to parse peer update interval, using default value %dms: %v", initialInterval, err)
   250	        } else {
   251	                initialInterval = int64(interval) * 10
   252	                go func() {
   253	                        startupPeriodStr := os.Getenv("NB_PEER_UPDATE_STARTUP_PERIOD_S")
   254	                        startupPeriod, err := strconv.Atoi(startupPeriodStr)
   255	                        if err != nil {
   256	                                startupPeriod = 1
   257	                                log.WithContext(ctx).Warnf("failed to parse peer update startup period, using default value %ds: %v", startupPeriod, err)
   258	                        }
   259	                        time.Sleep(time.Duration(startupPeriod) * time.Second)
   260	                        am.updateAccountPeersBufferInterval.Store(int64(time.Duration(interval) * time.Millisecond))
   261	                        log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("set peer update buffer interval to %dms", interval)
   262	                }()
   263	        }
   264	        am.updateAccountPeersBufferInterval.Store(initialInterval)
   265	        log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("set peer update buffer interval to %dms", initialInterval)
   266	
   267	}
   268

   270	        return am.externalCacheManager
   271	}

   274	        return am.idpManager

   277	// UpdateAccountSettings updates Account settings.
   278	// Only users with role UserRoleAdmin can update the account.
   279	// User that performs the update has to belong to the account.
   280	// Returns an updated Settings
   281	func (am *DefaultAccountManager) UpdateAccountSettings(ctx context.Context, accountID, userID string, newSettings *types.Settings) (*types.Settings, error) {
   282	        unlock := am.Store.AcquireWriteLockByUID(ctx, accountID)
   283	        defer unlock()
   284	
   285	        allowed, err := am.permissionsManager.ValidateUserPermissions(ctx, accountID, userID, modules.Settings, operations.Update)
   286	        if err != nil {
   287	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to validate user permissions: %w", err)
   288	        }
   289	
   290	        if !allowed {
   291	                return nil, status.NewPermissionDeniedError()
   292	        }
   293	
   294	        var oldSettings *types.Settings
   295	        var updateAccountPeers bool
   296	        var groupChangesAffectPeers bool
   297	
   298	        err = am.Store.ExecuteInTransaction(ctx, func(transaction store.Store) error {
   299	                var groupsUpdated bool
   300	
   301	                oldSettings, err = transaction.GetAccountSettings(ctx, store.LockingStrengthUpdate, accountID)
   302	                if err != nil {
   303	                        return err
   304	                }
   305	
   306	                if err = am.validateSettingsUpdate(ctx, transaction, newSettings, oldSettings, userID, accountID); err != nil {
   307	                        return err
   308	                }
   309	
   310	                if oldSettings.RoutingPeerDNSResolutionEnabled != newSettings.RoutingPeerDNSResolutionEnabled ||
   311	                        oldSettings.LazyConnectionEnabled != newSettings.LazyConnectionEnabled ||
   312	                        oldSettings.DNSDomain != newSettings.DNSDomain {
   313	                        updateAccountPeers = true
   314	                }
   315	
   316	                if oldSettings.GroupsPropagationEnabled != newSettings.GroupsPropagationEnabled && newSettings.GroupsPropagationEnabled {
   317	                        groupsUpdated, groupChangesAffectPeers, err = propagateUserGroupMemberships(ctx, transaction, accountID)
   318	                        if err != nil {
   319	                                return err
   320	                        }
   321	                }
   322	
   323	                if updateAccountPeers || groupsUpdated {
   324	                        if err = transaction.IncrementNetworkSerial(ctx, store.LockingStrengthUpdate, accountID); err != nil {
   325	                                return err
   326	                        }
   327	                }
   328	
   329	                return transaction.SaveAccountSettings(ctx, store.LockingStrengthUpdate, accountID, newSettings)
   330	        })
   331	        if err != nil {
   332	                return nil, err
   333	        }
   334	
   335	        extraSettingsChanged, err := am.settingsManager.UpdateExtraSettings(ctx, accountID, userID, newSettings.Extra)
   336	        if err != nil {
   337	                return nil, err
   338	        }
   339	
   340	        am.handleRoutingPeerDNSResolutionSettings(ctx, oldSettings, newSettings, userID, accountID)
   341	        am.handleLazyConnectionSettings(ctx, oldSettings, newSettings, userID, accountID)
   342	        am.handlePeerLoginExpirationSettings(ctx, oldSettings, newSettings, userID, accountID)
   343	        am.handleGroupsPropagationSettings(ctx, oldSettings, newSettings, userID, accountID)
   344	        if err = am.handleInactivityExpirationSettings(ctx, oldSettings, newSettings, userID, accountID); err != nil {
   345	                return nil, err
   346	        }
   347	        if oldSettings.DNSDomain != newSettings.DNSDomain {
   348	                am.StoreEvent(ctx, userID, accountID, accountID, activity.AccountDNSDomainUpdated, nil)
   349	        }
   350	
   351	        if updateAccountPeers || extraSettingsChanged || groupChangesAffectPeers {
   352	                go am.UpdateAccountPeers(ctx, accountID)
   353	        }
   354	
   355	        return newSettings, nil
   356	}
   357	
   358	func (am *DefaultAccountManager) validateSettingsUpdate(ctx context.Context, transaction store.Store, newSettings, oldSettings *types.Settings, userID, accountID string) error {
   359	        halfYearLimit := 180 * 24 * time.Hour
   360	        if newSettings.PeerLoginExpiration > halfYearLimit {
   361	                return status.Errorf(status.InvalidArgument, "peer login expiration can't be larger than 180 days")
   362	        }
   363	
   364	        if newSettings.PeerLoginExpiration < time.Hour {
   365	                return status.Errorf(status.InvalidArgument, "peer login expiration can't be smaller than one hour")
   366	        }
   367	
   368	        if newSettings.DNSDomain != "" && !isDomainValid(newSettings.DNSDomain) {
   369	                return status.Errorf(status.InvalidArgument, "invalid domain \"%s\" provided for DNS domain", newSettings.DNSDomain)
   370	        }
   371	
   372	        peers, err := transaction.GetAccountPeers(ctx, store.LockingStrengthShare, accountID, "", "")
   373	        if err != nil {
   374	                return err
   375	        }
   376	
   377	        peersMap := make(map[string]*nbpeer.Peer, len(peers))
   378	        for _, peer := range peers {
   379	                peersMap[peer.ID] = peer
   380	        }
   381	
   382	        return am.integratedPeerValidator.ValidateExtraSettings(ctx, newSettings.Extra, oldSettings.Extra, peersMap, userID, accountID)
   383	}
   384	
   385	func (am *DefaultAccountManager) handleRoutingPeerDNSResolutionSettings(ctx context.Context, oldSettings, newSettings *types.Settings, userID, accountID string) {
   386	        if oldSettings.RoutingPeerDNSResolutionEnabled != newSettings.RoutingPeerDNSResolutionEnabled {
   387	                if newSettings.RoutingPeerDNSResolutionEnabled {
   388	                        am.StoreEvent(ctx, userID, accountID, accountID, activity.AccountRoutingPeerDNSResolutionEnabled, nil)
   389	                } else {
   390	                        am.StoreEvent(ctx, userID, accountID, accountID, activity.AccountRoutingPeerDNSResolutionDisabled, nil)
   391	                }
   392	        }
   393	}
   394	
   395	func (am *DefaultAccountManager) handleLazyConnectionSettings(ctx context.Context, oldSettings, newSettings *types.Settings, userID, accountID string) {
   396	        if oldSettings.LazyConnectionEnabled != newSettings.LazyConnectionEnabled {
   397	                if newSettings.LazyConnectionEnabled {
   398	                        am.StoreEvent(ctx, userID, accountID, accountID, activity.AccountLazyConnectionEnabled, nil)
   399	                } else {
   400	                        am.StoreEvent(ctx, userID, accountID, accountID, activity.AccountLazyConnectionDisabled, nil)
   401	                }
   402	        }
   403	}
   404	
   405	func (am *DefaultAccountManager) handlePeerLoginExpirationSettings(ctx context.Context, oldSettings, newSettings *types.Settings, userID, accountID string) {
   406	        if oldSettings.PeerLoginExpirationEnabled != newSettings.PeerLoginExpirationEnabled {
   407	                event := activity.AccountPeerLoginExpirationEnabled
   408	                if !newSettings.PeerLoginExpirationEnabled {
   409	                        event = activity.AccountPeerLoginExpirationDisabled
   410	                        am.peerLoginExpiry.Cancel(ctx, []string{accountID})
   411	                } else {
   412	                        am.checkAndSchedulePeerLoginExpiration(ctx, accountID)
   413	                }
   414	                am.StoreEvent(ctx, userID, accountID, accountID, event, nil)
   415	        }
   416	
   417	        if oldSettings.PeerLoginExpiration != newSettings.PeerLoginExpiration {
   418	                am.StoreEvent(ctx, userID, accountID, accountID, activity.AccountPeerLoginExpirationDurationUpdated, nil)

  1732	// Returns the list of standard auto groups and a map of JWT auto groups,
  1733	// where the keys are the group names and the values are the group IDs.
  1734	func separateGroups(autoGroups []string, allGroups []*types.Group) ([]string, map[string]string) {
  1735	        newAutoGroups := make([]string, 0)
  1736	        jwtAutoGroups := make(map[string]string) // map of group name to group ID
  1737	
  1738	        allGroupsMap := make(map[string]*types.Group, len(allGroups))
  1739	        for _, group := range allGroups {
  1740	                allGroupsMap[group.ID] = group
  1741	        }
  1742	
  1743	        for _, id := range autoGroups {
  1744	                if group, ok := allGroupsMap[id]; ok {
  1745	                        if group.Issued == types.GroupIssuedJWT {
  1746	                                jwtAutoGroups[group.Name] = id
  1747	                        } else {
  1748	                                newAutoGroups = append(newAutoGroups, id)
  1749	                        }
  1750	                }
  1751	        }
  1752	
  1753	        return newAutoGroups, jwtAutoGroups
  1754	}

   306	
   307	                        if !disableMetrics {
   308	                                idpManager := "disabled"
   309	                                if config.IdpManagerConfig != nil && config.IdpManagerConfig.ManagerType != "" {
   310	                                        idpManager = config.IdpManagerConfig.ManagerType
   311	                                }
   312	                                metricsWorker := metrics.NewWorker(ctx, installationID, store, peersUpdateManager, idpManager)
   313	                                go metricsWorker.Run(ctx)
   314	                        }
   315	
   316	                        var compatListener net.Listener
   317	                        if mgmtPort != ManagementLegacyPort {
   318	                                // The Management gRPC server was running on port 33073 previously. Old agents that are already connected to it
   319	                                // are using port 33073. For compatibility purposes we keep running a 2nd gRPC server on port 33073.
   320	                                compatListener, err = serveGRPC(ctx, gRPCAPIHandler, ManagementLegacyPort)
   321	                                if err != nil {
   322	                                        return err
   323	                                }
   324	                                log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("running gRPC backward compatibility server: %s", compatListener.Addr().String())
   325	                        }
   326	
   327	                        rootHandler := handlerFunc(gRPCAPIHandler, httpAPIHandler)
   328	                        var listener net.Listener
   329	                        if certManager != nil {
   330	                                // a call to certManager.Listener() always creates a new listener so we do it once
   331	                                cml := certManager.Listener()
   332	                                if mgmtPort == 443 {
   333	                                        // CertManager, HTTP and gRPC API all on the same port
   334	                                        rootHandler = certManager.HTTPHandler(rootHandler)
   335	                                        listener = cml
   336	                                } else {
   337	                                        listener, err = tls.Listen("tcp", fmt.Sprintf(":%d", mgmtPort), certManager.TLSConfig())
   338	                                        if err != nil {
   339	                                                return fmt.Errorf("failed creating TLS listener on port %d: %v", mgmtPort, err)
   340	                                        }
   341	                                        log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("running HTTP server (LetsEncrypt challenge handler): %s", cml.Addr().String())
   342	                                        serveHTTP(ctx, cml, certManager.HTTPHandler(nil))
   343	                                }
   344	                        } else if tlsConfig != nil {
   345	                                listener, err = tls.Listen("tcp", fmt.Sprintf(":%d", mgmtPort), tlsConfig)
   346	                                if err != nil {
   347	                                        return fmt.Errorf("failed creating TLS listener on port %d: %v", mgmtPort, err)
   348	                                }
   349	                        } else {
   350	                                listener, err = net.Listen("tcp", fmt.Sprintf(":%d", mgmtPort))
   351	                                if err != nil {
   352	                                        return fmt.Errorf("failed creating TCP listener on port %d: %v", mgmtPort, err)
   353	                                }
   354	                        }
   355	
   356	                        log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("management server version %s", version.NetbirdVersion())
   357	                        log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("running HTTP server and gRPC server on the same port: %s", listener.Addr().String())
   358	                        serveGRPCWithHTTP(ctx, listener, rootHandler, tlsEnabled)
   359	
   360	                        SetupCloseHandler()
   361	
   362	                        <-stopCh
   363	                        integratedPeerValidator.Stop(ctx)
   364	                        if geo != nil {
   365	                                _ = geo.Stop()
   366	                        }
   367	                        ephemeralManager.Stop()
   368	                        _ = appMetrics.Close()
   369	                        _ = listener.Close()
   370	                        if certManager != nil {
   371	                                _ = certManager.Listener().Close()
   372	                        }
   373	                        gRPCAPIHandler.Stop()
   374	                        _ = store.Close(ctx)
   375	                        _ = eventStore.Close(ctx)
   376	                        log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("stopped Management Service")
   377	
   378	                        return nil
   379	                },
   380	        }
   381	)
   382	
   383	func unaryInterceptor(
   384	        ctx context.Context,
   385	        req interface{},
   386	        info *grpc.UnaryServerInfo,
   387	        handler grpc.UnaryHandler,
   388	) (interface{}, error) {
   389	        reqID := uuid.New().String()
   390	        //nolint
   391	        ctx = context.WithValue(ctx, hook.ExecutionContextKey, hook.GRPCSource)
   392	        //nolint
   393	        ctx = context.WithValue(ctx, nbContext.RequestIDKey, reqID)
   394	        return handler(ctx, req)
   395	}
   396	
   397	func streamInterceptor(
   398	        srv interface{},
   399	        ss grpc.ServerStream,
   400	        info *grpc.StreamServerInfo,
   401	        handler grpc.StreamHandler,
   402	) error {
   403	        reqID := uuid.New().String()
   404	        wrapped := grpcMiddleware.WrapServerStream(ss)
   405	        //nolint
   406	        ctx := context.WithValue(ss.Context(), hook.ExecutionContextKey, hook.GRPCSource)
   407	        //nolint
   408	        wrapped.WrappedContext = context.WithValue(ctx, nbContext.RequestIDKey, reqID)
   409	        return handler(srv, wrapped)
   410	}
   411	
   412	func notifyStop(ctx context.Context, msg string) {
   413	        select {
   414	        case stopCh <- 1:
   415	                log.WithContext(ctx).Error(msg)
   416	        default:
   417	                // stop has been already called, nothing to report
   418	        }
   419	}
   420	
   421	func getInstallationID(ctx context.Context, store store.Store) (string, error) {
   422	        installationID := store.GetInstallationID()
   423	        if installationID != "" {
   424	                return installationID, nil
   425	        }
   426	
   427	        installationID = strings.ToUpper(uuid.New().String())
   428	        err := store.SaveInstallationID(ctx, installationID)
   429	        if err != nil {
   430	                return "", err
   431	        }
   432	        return installationID, nil
   433	}
   434	
   435	func serveGRPC(ctx context.Context, grpcServer *grpc.Server, port int) (net.Listener, error) {
   436	        listener, err := net.Listen("tcp", fmt.Sprintf(":%d", port))
   437	        if err != nil {
   438	                return nil, err
   439	        }
   440	        go func() {
   441	                err := grpcServer.Serve(listener)
   442	                if err != nil {
   443	                        notifyStop(ctx, fmt.Sprintf("failed running gRPC server on port %d: %v", port, err))
   444	                }
   445	        }()
   446	        return listener, nil
   447	}

    84	// SetupCloseHandler handles SIGTERM signal and exits with success
    85	func SetupCloseHandler() {
    86	        c := make(chan os.Signal, 1)
    87	        signal.Notify(c, os.Interrupt)
    88	        go func() {
    89	                for range c {
    90	                        fmt.Println("\r- Ctrl+C pressed in Terminal")
    91	                        stopCh <- 0
    92	                }
    93	        }()
    94	}

    58	// GetAuthAudiences returns the audience from the http config and device authorization flow config
    59	func (c Config) GetAuthAudiences() []string {
    60	        audiences := []string{c.HttpConfig.AuthAudience}
    61	
    62	        if c.HttpConfig.ExtraAuthAudience != "" {
    63	                audiences = append(audiences, c.HttpConfig.ExtraAuthAudience)
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        if c.DeviceAuthorizationFlow != nil && c.DeviceAuthorizationFlow.ProviderConfig.Audience != "" {
    67	                audiences = append(audiences, c.DeviceAuthorizationFlow.ProviderConfig.Audience)
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        return audiences
    71	}

   103	
   104	// GetRoutesToSync returns the enabled routes for the peer ID and the routes
   105	// from the ACL peers that have distribution groups associated with the peer ID.
   106	// Please mind, that the returned route.Route objects will contain Peer.Key instead of Peer.ID.
   107	func (a *Account) GetRoutesToSync(ctx context.Context, peerID string, aclPeers []*nbpeer.Peer) []*route.Route {
   108	        routes, peerDisabledRoutes := a.getRoutingPeerRoutes(ctx, peerID)
   109	        peerRoutesMembership := make(LookupMap)
   110	        for _, r := range append(routes, peerDisabledRoutes...) {
   111	                peerRoutesMembership[string(r.GetHAUniqueID())] = struct{}{}
   112	        }
   113	
   114	        groupListMap := a.GetPeerGroups(peerID)
   115	        for _, peer := range aclPeers {
   116	                activeRoutes, _ := a.getRoutingPeerRoutes(ctx, peer.ID)
   117	                groupFilteredRoutes := a.filterRoutesByGroups(activeRoutes, groupListMap)
   118	                filteredRoutes := a.filterRoutesFromPeersOfSameHAGroup(groupFilteredRoutes, peerRoutesMembership)
   119	                routes = append(routes, filteredRoutes...)
   120	        }
   121	
   122	        return routes
   123	}
   124	
   125	// filterRoutesFromPeersOfSameHAGroup filters and returns a list of routes that don't share the same HA route membership
   126	func (a *Account) filterRoutesFromPeersOfSameHAGroup(routes []*route.Route, peerMemberships LookupMap) []*route.Route {
   127	        var filteredRoutes []*route.Route
   128	        for _, r := range routes {
   129	                _, found := peerMemberships[string(r.GetHAUniqueID())]
   130	                if !found {
   131	                        filteredRoutes = append(filteredRoutes, r)
   132	                }
   133	        }
   134	        return filteredRoutes
   135	}
   136	
   137	// filterRoutesByGroups returns a list with routes that have distribution groups in the group's map
   138	func (a *Account) filterRoutesByGroups(routes []*route.Route, groupListMap LookupMap) []*route.Route {
   139	        var filteredRoutes []*route.Route
   140	        for _, r := range routes {
   141	                for _, groupID := range r.Groups {
   142	                        _, found := groupListMap[groupID]
   143	                        if found {
   144	                                filteredRoutes = append(filteredRoutes, r)
   145	                                break
   146	                        }
   147	                }
   148	        }
   149	        return filteredRoutes
   150	}

import (
	"fmt"
	"github.com/netbirdio/netbird/management/server/types"
)

func main() {
	// Test 1: Account creation with default policy (current behavior)
	fmt.Println("Test 1: Creating account with default behavior...")
	account1 := types.Account{
		Id:       "test-account-1",
		CreatedBy: "test-user",
		Domain:   "test.domain",
		Groups:   make(map[string]*types.Group),
		Policies: nil,
	}
	
	err := account1.AddAllGroup()
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error adding all group: %v\n", err)
		return
	}
	
	fmt.Printf("Account 1 Groups: %d\n", len(account1.Groups))
	fmt.Printf("Account 1 Policies: %d\n", len(account1.Policies))
	if len(account1.Policies) > 0 {
		fmt.Printf("Policy Name: %s\n", account1.Policies[0].Name)
		fmt.Printf("Policy Description: %s\n", account1.Policies[0].Description)
	}
	
	fmt.Println("\nTest completed successfully!")
}'

' --new_str '// AddAllGroup to account object if it doesn'"'"'t exist
// If createDefaultPolicy is false, only the "All" group will be created without the default policy
func (a *Account) AddAllGroup(createDefaultPolicy bool) error {
	if len(a.Groups) == 0 {
		allGroup := &Group{
			ID:     xid.New().String(),
			Name:   "All",
			Issued: GroupIssuedAPI,
		}
		for _, peer := range a.Peers {
			allGroup.Peers = append(allGroup.Peers, peer.ID)
		}
		a.Groups = map[string]*Group{allGroup.ID: allGroup}

		if createDefaultPolicy {
			id := xid.New().String()

			defaultPolicy := &Policy{
				ID:          id,
				Name:        DefaultRuleName,
				Description: DefaultRuleDescription,
				Enabled:     true,
				Rules: []*PolicyRule{
					{
						ID:            id,
						Name:          DefaultRuleName,
						Description:   DefaultRuleDescription,
						Enabled:       true,
						Sources:       []string{allGroup.ID},
						Destinations:  []string{allGroup.ID},
						Bidirectional: true,
						Protocol:      PolicyRuleProtocolALL,
						Action:        PolicyTrafficActionAccept,
					},
				},
			}

			a.Policies = []*Policy{defaultPolicy}
		}
	}
	return nil
}

🎬 ACTION
cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/addall_patch.go << 'ENDPATCH'
// AddAllGroup to account object if it doesn't exist
// If createDefaultPolicy is false, only the "All" group will be created without the default policy
func (a *Account) AddAllGroup(createDefaultPolicy bool) error {
	if len(a.Groups) == 0 {
		allGroup := &Group{
			ID:     xid.New().String(),
			Name:   "All",
			Issued: GroupIssuedAPI,
		}
		for _, peer := range a.Peers {
			allGroup.Peers = append(allGroup.Peers, peer.ID)
		}
		a.Groups = map[string]*Group{allGroup.ID: allGroup}

		if createDefaultPolicy {
			id := xid.New().String()

			defaultPolicy := &Policy{
				ID:          id,
				Name:        DefaultRuleName,
				Description: DefaultRuleDescription,
				Enabled:     true,
				Rules: []*PolicyRule{
					{
						ID:            id,
						Name:          DefaultRuleName,
						Description:   DefaultRuleDescription,
						Enabled:       true,
						Sources:       []string{allGroup.ID},
						Destinations:  []string{allGroup.ID},
						Bidirectional: true,
						Protocol:      PolicyRuleProtocolALL,
						Action:        PolicyTrafficActionAccept,
					},
				},
			}

			a.Policies = []*Policy{defaultPolicy}
		}
	}
	return nil
}
ENDPATCH

// AddAllGroup to account object if it doesn't exist
// If createDefaultPolicy is false, only the "All" group will be created without the default policy
func (a *Account) AddAllGroup(createDefaultPolicy bool) error {
if len(a.Groups) == 0 {
allGroup := &Group{
ID:     xid.New().String(),
Name:   "All",
Issued: GroupIssuedAPI,
}
for _, peer := range a.Peers {
allGroup.Peers = append(allGroup.Peers, peer.ID)
}
a.Groups = map[string]*Group{allGroup.ID: allGroup}

if createDefaultPolicy {
id := xid.New().String()

defaultPolicy := &Policy{
ID:          id,
Name:        DefaultRuleName,
Description: DefaultRuleDescription,
Enabled:     true,
Rules: []*PolicyRule{
{
ID:            id,
Name:          DefaultRuleName,
Description:   DefaultRuleDescription,
Enabled:       true,
Sources:       []string{allGroup.ID},
Destinations:  []string{allGroup.ID},
Bidirectional: true,
Protocol:      PolicyRuleProtocolALL,
Action:        PolicyTrafficActionAccept,
},
},
}

a.Policies = []*Policy{defaultPolicy}
}
}
return nil
}

cd /testbed && python3 << 'ENDPY'
import re

# Read the file
with open('/testbed/management/server/types/account.go', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Find and replace the AddAllGroup function
old_pattern = r'// AddAllGroup to account object if it doesn\'t exist\nfunc \(a \*Account\) AddAllGroup\(\) error \{'
new_pattern = '// AddAllGroup to account object if it doesn\'t exist\n// If createDefaultPolicy is false, only the "All" group will be created without the default policy\nfunc (a *Account) AddAllGroup(createDefaultPolicy bool) error {'

content = content.replace(
    '// AddAllGroup to account object if it doesn\'t exist\nfunc (a *Account) AddAllGroup() error {',
    '// AddAllGroup to account object if it doesn\'t exist\n// If createDefaultPolicy is false, only the "All" group will be created without the default policy\nfunc (a *Account) AddAllGroup(createDefaultPolicy bool) error {'
)

# Now wrap the default policy creation in an if statement
old_block = '''		a.Groups = map[string]*Group{allGroup.ID: allGroup}

		id := xid.New().String()

		defaultPolicy := &Policy{
			ID:          id,
			Name:        DefaultRuleName,
			Description: DefaultRuleDescription,
			Enabled:     true,
			Rules: []*PolicyRule{
				{
					ID:            id,
					Name:          DefaultRuleName,
					Description:   DefaultRuleDescription,
					Enabled:       true,
					Sources:       []string{allGroup.ID},
					Destinations:  []string{allGroup.ID},
					Bidirectional: true,
					Protocol:      PolicyRuleProtocolALL,
					Action:        PolicyTrafficActionAccept,
				},
			},
		}

		a.Policies = []*Policy{defaultPolicy}'''

new_block = '''		a.Groups = map[string]*Group{allGroup.ID: allGroup}

		if createDefaultPolicy {
			id := xid.New().String()

			defaultPolicy := &Policy{
				ID:          id,
				Name:        DefaultRuleName,
				Description: DefaultRuleDescription,
				Enabled:     true,
				Rules: []*PolicyRule{
					{
						ID:            id,
						Name:          DefaultRuleName,
						Description:   DefaultRuleDescription,
						Enabled:       true,
						Sources:       []string{allGroup.ID},
						Destinations:  []string{allGroup.ID},
						Bidirectional: true,
						Protocol:      PolicyRuleProtocolALL,
						Action:        PolicyTrafficActionAccept,
					},
				},
			}

			a.Policies = []*Policy{defaultPolicy}
		}'''

content = content.replace(old_block, new_block)

# Write the modified content back
with open('/testbed/management/server/types/account.go', 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)

print("Successfully modified account.go")
ENDPY

# Read the file
with open('/testbed/management/server/types/account.go', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Find and replace the AddAllGroup function
old_pattern = r'// AddAllGroup to account object if it doesn\'t exist\nfunc \(a \*Account\) AddAllGroup\(\) error \{'
new_pattern = '// AddAllGroup to account object if it doesn\'t exist\n// If createDefaultPolicy is false, only the "All" group will be created without the default policy\nfunc (a *Account) AddAllGroup(createDefaultPolicy bool) error {'

content = content.replace(
    '// AddAllGroup to account object if it doesn\'t exist\nfunc (a *Account) AddAllGroup() error {',
    '// AddAllGroup to account object if it doesn\'t exist\n// If createDefaultPolicy is false, only the "All" group will be created without the default policy\nfunc (a *Account) AddAllGroup(createDefaultPolicy bool) error {'
)

# Now wrap the default policy creation in an if statement
old_block = '''		a.Groups = map[string]*Group{allGroup.ID: allGroup}

		id := xid.New().String()

		defaultPolicy := &Policy{
			ID:          id,
			Name:        DefaultRuleName,
			Description: DefaultRuleDescription,
			Enabled:     true,
			Rules: []*PolicyRule{
				{
					ID:            id,
					Name:          DefaultRuleName,
					Description:   DefaultRuleDescription,
					Enabled:       true,
					Sources:       []string{allGroup.ID},
					Destinations:  []string{allGroup.ID},
					Bidirectional: true,
					Protocol:      PolicyRuleProtocolALL,
					Action:        PolicyTrafficActionAccept,
				},
			},
		}

		a.Policies = []*Policy{defaultPolicy}'''

new_block = '''		a.Groups = map[string]*Group{allGroup.ID: allGroup}

		if createDefaultPolicy {
			id := xid.New().String()

			defaultPolicy := &Policy{
				ID:          id,
				Name:        DefaultRuleName,
				Description: DefaultRuleDescription,
				Enabled:     true,
				Rules: []*PolicyRule{
					{
						ID:            id,
						Name:          DefaultRuleName,
						Description:   DefaultRuleDescription,
						Enabled:       true,
						Sources:       []string{allGroup.ID},
						Destinations:  []string{allGroup.ID},

						Protocol:      PolicyRuleProtocolALL,
						Action:        PolicyTrafficActionAccept,
					},
				},
			}

			a.Policies = []*Policy{defaultPolicy}
		}'''

content = content.replace(old_block, new_block)

    f.write(content)

import re

# Read the file
with open('/testbed/management/server/types/account.go', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Find and replace the AddAllGroup function
old_pattern = r'// AddAllGroup to account object if it doesn\'t exist\nfunc \(a \*Account\) AddAllGroup\(\) error \{'
new_pattern = '// AddAllGroup to account object if it doesn\'t exist\n// If createDefaultPolicy is false, only the "All" group will be created without the default policy\nfunc (a *Account) AddAllGroup(createDefaultPolicy bool) error {'

content = content.replace(
    '// AddAllGroup to account object if it doesn\'t exist\nfunc (a *Account) AddAllGroup() error {',
    '// AddAllGroup to account object if it doesn\'t exist\n// If createDefaultPolicy is false, only the "All" group will be created without the default policy\nfunc (a *Account) AddAllGroup(createDefaultPolicy bool) error {'
)

# Now wrap the default policy creation in an if statement
old_block = '''		a.Groups = map[string]*Group{allGroup.ID: allGroup}

		id := xid.New().String()

		defaultPolicy := &Policy{
			ID:          id,
			Name:        DefaultRuleName,
			Description: DefaultRuleDescription,
			Enabled:     true,
			Rules: []*PolicyRule{
				{
					ID:            id,
					Name:          DefaultRuleName,
					Description:   DefaultRuleDescription,
					Enabled:       true,
					Sources:       []string{allGroup.ID},
					Destinations:  []string{allGroup.ID},
					Bidirectional: true,
					Protocol:      PolicyRuleProtocolALL,
					Action:        PolicyTrafficActionAccept,
				},
			},
		}

		a.Policies = []*Policy{defaultPolicy}'''

new_block = '''		a.Groups = map[string]*Group{allGroup.ID: allGroup}

		if createDefaultPolicy {
			id := xid.New().String()

			defaultPolicy := &Policy{
				ID:          id,
				Name:        DefaultRuleName,
				Description: DefaultRuleDescription,
				Enabled:     true,
				Rules: []*PolicyRule{
					{
						ID:            id,
						Name:          DefaultRuleName,
						Description:   DefaultRuleDescription,
						Enabled:       true,
						Sources:       []string{allGroup.ID},
						Destinations:  []string{allGroup.ID},
						Bidirectional: true,
						Protocol:      PolicyRuleProtocolALL,
						Action:        PolicyTrafficActionAccept,
					},
				},
			}

			a.Policies = []*Policy{defaultPolicy}
		}'''

content = content.replace(old_block, new_block)

# Write the modified content back
with open('/testbed/management/server/types/account.go', 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)

print("Successfully modified account.go")

OBSERVATION:

	for i := 0; i < 2; i++ {
		accountId := xid.New().String()

		_, err := am.Store.GetAccount(ctx, accountId)
		statusErr, _ := status.FromError(err)
		switch {
		case err == nil:
			log.WithContext(ctx).Warnf("an account with ID already exists, retrying...")
			continue
		case statusErr.Type() == status.NotFound:
			newAccount := newAccountWithId(ctx, accountId, userID, domain)
			am.StoreEvent(ctx, userID, newAccount.Id, accountId, activity.AccountCreated, nil)
			return newAccount, nil
		default:
			return nil, err
		}
	}

	return nil, status.Errorf(status.Internal, "error while creating new account")
}

import re

# Read the account.go file
with open('/testbed/management/server/account.go', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

# 1. Update newAccountWithId function signature
content = content.replace(
    'func newAccountWithId(ctx context.Context, accountID, userID, domain string) *types.Account {',
    'func newAccountWithId(ctx context.Context, accountID, userID, domain string, disableDefaultAllPolicy bool) *types.Account {'
)

# 2. Update the call to AddAllGroup in newAccountWithId
content = content.replace(
    '\tif err := acc.AddAllGroup(); err != nil {',
    '\tif err := acc.AddAllGroup(!disableDefaultAllPolicy); err != nil {'
)

# 3. Update the call to newAccountWithId in newAccount method
content = content.replace(
    '\t\t\tnewAccount := newAccountWithId(ctx, accountId, userID, domain)',
    '\t\t\tnewAccount := newAccountWithId(ctx, accountId, userID, domain, am.disableDefaultAllPolicy)'
)

# 4. Update other places that call newAccountWithId (in GetOrCreateAccountByPrivateDomain)
# Find and update the pattern - this requires more careful handling
old_pattern = r'newAccount := &types\.Account\{(.*?)\}'
matches = list(re.finditer(old_pattern, content, re.DOTALL))
for match in matches:
    # Check if AddAllGroup is called after this
    end_pos = match.end()
    next_chunk = content[end_pos:end_pos+200]
    if 'AddAllGroup()' in next_chunk:
        # Update the AddAllGroup call
        content = content[end_pos:end_pos+200].replace('AddAllGroup()', 'AddAllGroup(true)', 1)
        content = content[:end_pos] + content[end_pos:end_pos+200].replace('AddAllGroup()', 'AddAllGroup(true)', 1) + content[end_pos+200:]

# Write the modified content back
with open('/testbed/management/server/account.go', 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)

print("Successfully updated account.go")
ENDPY

# Read the account.go file
with open('/testbed/management/server/account.go', 'r') as f:
    lines = f.readlines()

# Find and update the newAccountWithId function signature
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    if 'func newAccountWithId(ctx context.Context, accountID, userID, domain string) *types.Account {' in line:
        lines[i] = line.replace(
            'func newAccountWithId(ctx context.Context, accountID, userID, domain string) *types.Account {',
            'func newAccountWithId(ctx context.Context, accountID, userID, domain string, disableDefaultAllPolicy bool) *types.Account {'
        )
    elif '\tif err := acc.AddAllGroup(); err != nil {' in line:
        lines[i] = line.replace(
            '\tif err := acc.AddAllGroup(); err != nil {',
            '\tif err := acc.AddAllGroup(!disableDefaultAllPolicy); err != nil {'
        )
    elif '\t\t\tnewAccount := newAccountWithId(ctx, accountId, userID, domain)' in line:
        lines[i] = line.replace(
            '\t\t\tnewAccount := newAccountWithId(ctx, accountId, userID, domain)',
            '\t\t\tnewAccount := newAccountWithId(ctx, accountId, userID, domain, am.disableDefaultAllPolicy)'
        )
    elif '\t\tif err := newAccount.AddAllGroup(); err != nil {' in line:
        lines[i] = line.replace(
            '\t\tif err := newAccount.AddAllGroup(); err != nil {',
            '\t\tif err := newAccount.AddAllGroup(true); err != nil {'
        )

# Write the modified content back
with open('/testbed/management/server/account.go', 'w') as f:
    f.writelines(lines)

print("Successfully updated account.go")

import (

	"github.com/netbirdio/netbird/management/server/types"
)

func main() {
	ctx := context.Background()
	
	// Test 1: Creating account with default policy enabled (backward compatible)
	fmt.Println("Test 1: Account with default policy enabled")
	account1 := types.Account{
		Id:        "test-account-1",
		CreatedBy: "test-user",
		Domain:    "test.domain",
		Groups:    make(map[string]*types.Group),
		Policies:  nil,
	}
	
	if err := account1.AddAllGroup(true); err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error adding all group: %v\n", err)
		return
	}
	
	fmt.Printf("Groups created: %d\n", len(account1.Groups))
	fmt.Printf("Policies created: %d\n", len(account1.Policies))
	if len(account1.Policies) > 0 {
		fmt.Printf("Policy Name: %s\n", account1.Policies[0].Name)
	}
	
	// Test 2: Creating account with default policy disabled
	fmt.Println("\nTest 2: Account with default policy disabled")
	account2 := types.Account{
		Id:        "test-account-2",
		CreatedBy: "test-user",
		Domain:    "test.domain",
		Groups:    make(map[string]*types.Group),
		Policies:  nil,
	}
	
	if err := account2.AddAllGroup(false); err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error adding all group: %v\n", err)
		return
	}
	
	fmt.Printf("Groups created: %d\n", len(account2.Groups))
	fmt.Printf("Policies created: %d\n", len(account2.Policies))
	if len(account2.Policies) == 0 {
		fmt.Println("✓ No default policy created as expected!")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("✗ Default policy was created unexpectedly!")
	}
	
	fmt.Println("\nAll tests completed successfully!")
}

func (a *Account) AddAllGroup(createDefaultPolicy bool) error {
	if len(a.Groups) == 0 {
		allGroup := &Group{
			ID:     xid.New().String(),
			Name:   "All",
			Issued: GroupIssuedAPI,
		}
		for _, peer := range a.Peers {
			allGroup.Peers = append(allGroup.Peers, peer.ID)
		}
		a.Groups = map[string]*Group{allGroup.ID: allGroup}

		id := xid.New().String()

		defaultPolicy := &Policy{
			ID:          id,
			Name:        DefaultRuleName,
			Description: DefaultRuleDescription,
			Enabled:     true,
			Rules: []*PolicyRule{
				{
					ID:            id,
					Name:          DefaultRuleName,
					Description:   DefaultRuleDescription,
					Enabled:       true,
					Sources:       []string{allGroup.ID},
					Destinations:  []string{allGroup.ID},
					Bidirectional: true,
					Protocol:      PolicyRuleProtocolALL,
					Action:        PolicyTrafficActionAccept,
				},
			},
		}

		a.Policies = []*Policy{defaultPolicy}
	}
	return nil
}

func (a *Account) AddAllGroup(createDefaultPolicy bool) error {
	if len(a.Groups) == 0 {
		allGroup := &Group{
			ID:     xid.New().String(),
			Name:   "All",
			Issued: GroupIssuedAPI,
		}
		for _, peer := range a.Peers {
			allGroup.Peers = append(allGroup.Peers, peer.ID)
		}
		a.Groups = map[string]*Group{allGroup.ID: allGroup}

		id := xid.New().String()

		defaultPolicy := &Policy{
			ID:          id,
			Name:        DefaultRuleName,
			Description: DefaultRuleDescription,
			Enabled:     true,
			Rules: []*PolicyRule{
				{
					ID:            id,
					Name:          DefaultRuleName,
					Description:   DefaultRuleDescription,
					Enabled:       true,
					Sources:       []string{allGroup.ID},
					Destinations:  []string{allGroup.ID},
					Bidirectional: true,
					Protocol:      PolicyRuleProtocolALL,
					Action:        PolicyTrafficActionAccept,
				},
			},
		}

		a.Policies = []*Policy{defaultPolicy}
	}
	return nil
}

# Read the file
with open('/testbed/management/server/types/account.go', 'r') as f:
    lines = f.readlines()

# Find the line that has "a.Groups = map[string]*Group{allGroup.ID: allGroup}" and insert "if createDefaultPolicy {" after it
modified_lines = []
i = 0
while i < len(lines):
    modified_lines.append(lines[i])
    # Check if this is the line after which we need to add the if statement
    if '\t\ta.Groups = map[string]*Group{allGroup.ID: allGroup}' in lines[i]:
        # Add an empty line and then the if statement
        modified_lines.append('\n')
        modified_lines.append('\t\tif createDefaultPolicy {\n')
        # Find the line with "a.Policies = []*Policy{defaultPolicy}" and add a closing brace after it
        # For now, let's just mark that we've added the opening brace
        i += 1
        # Now copy lines until we find a.Policies line, and indent them
        while i < len(lines) and 'a.Policies = []*Policy{defaultPolicy}' not in lines[i]:
            # Indent the line by one more tab
            if lines[i].startswith('\t\t'):
                modified_lines.append('\t' + lines[i])
            else:
                modified_lines.append(lines[i])
            i += 1
        # Add the a.Policies line with extra indentation
        if i < len(lines):
            modified_lines.append('\t' + lines[i])
            # Add the closing brace
            modified_lines.append('\t\t}\n')
    i += 1

# Write back
with open('/testbed/management/server/types/account.go', 'w') as f:
    f.writelines(modified_lines)

print("Successfully updated types/account.go with if statement")

func (a *Account) AddAllGroup(createDefaultPolicy bool) error {
	if len(a.Groups) == 0 {
		allGroup := &Group{
			ID:     xid.New().String(),
			Name:   "All",
			Issued: GroupIssuedAPI,
		}
		for _, peer := range a.Peers {
			allGroup.Peers = append(allGroup.Peers, peer.ID)
		}
		a.Groups = map[string]*Group{allGroup.ID: allGroup}

		if createDefaultPolicy {

			id := xid.New().String()

			defaultPolicy := &Policy{
				ID:          id,
				Name:        DefaultRuleName,
				Description: DefaultRuleDescription,
				Enabled:     true,
				Rules: []*PolicyRule{
					{
						ID:            id,
						Name:          DefaultRuleName,
						Description:   DefaultRuleDescription,
						Enabled:       true,
						Sources:       []string{allGroup.ID},
						Destinations:  []string{allGroup.ID},
						Bidirectional: true,
						Protocol:      PolicyRuleProtocolALL,
						Action:        PolicyTrafficActionAccept,
					},
				},
			}

			a.Policies = []*Policy{defaultPolicy}
		}
	}
	return nil
}

+package main
+
+import (
+"fmt"
+"github.com/netbirdio/netbird/management/server/types"
+)
+
+func main() {
+// Test 1: Account creation with default policy (current behavior)
+fmt.Println("Test 1: Creating account with default behavior...")
+account1 := types.Account{
+Id:       "test-account-1",
+CreatedBy: "test-user",
+Domain:   "test.domain",
+Groups:   make(map[string]*types.Group),
+Policies: nil,
+}
+
+err := account1.AddAllGroup()
+if err != nil {
+fmt.Printf("Error adding all group: %v\n", err)
+return
+}
+
+fmt.Printf("Account 1 Groups: %d\n", len(account1.Groups))
+fmt.Printf("Account 1 Policies: %d\n", len(account1.Policies))
+if len(account1.Policies) > 0 {
+fmt.Printf("Policy Name: %s\n", account1.Policies[0].Name)
+fmt.Printf("Policy Description: %s\n", account1.Policies[0].Description)
+}
+
+fmt.Println("\nTest completed successfully!")
+}

@@ -0,0 +1,56 @@
+package main
+
+import (
+"fmt"
+
+"github.com/netbirdio/netbird/management/server/types"
+)
+
+func main() {
+
+// Test 1: Creating account with default policy enabled (backward compatible)
+fmt.Println("Test 1: Account with default policy enabled")
+account1 := types.Account{
+Id:        "test-account-1",
+CreatedBy: "test-user",
+Domain:    "test.domain",
+Groups:    make(map[string]*types.Group),
+Policies:  nil,
+}
+
+if err := account1.AddAllGroup(true); err != nil {
+fmt.Printf("Error adding all group: %v\n", err)
+return
+}
+
+fmt.Printf("Groups created: %d\n", len(account1.Groups))
+fmt.Printf("Policies created: %d\n", len(account1.Policies))
+if len(account1.Policies) > 0 {
+fmt.Printf("Policy Name: %s\n", account1.Policies[0].Name)
+}
+
+// Test 2: Creating account with default policy disabled
+fmt.Println("\nTest 2: Account with default policy disabled")
+account2 := types.Account{
+Id:        "test-account-2",
+CreatedBy: "test-user",
+Domain:    "test.domain",
+Groups:    make(map[string]*types.Group),
+Policies:  nil,
+}
+
+if err := account2.AddAllGroup(false); err != nil {
+fmt.Printf("Error adding all group: %v\n", err)
+return
+}
+
+fmt.Printf("Groups created: %d\n", len(account2.Groups))
+fmt.Printf("Policies created: %d\n", len(account2.Policies))
+if len(account2.Policies) == 0 {
+fmt.Println("✓ No default policy created as expected!")
+} else {
+fmt.Println("✗ Default policy was created unexpectedly!")
+}
+
+fmt.Println("\nAll tests completed successfully!")
+}
